***говаривать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говаривать.html>гова́ривать</a> (10272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говаривать.html>гова́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to say <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говаривать.html>гова́ривал</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on částo <b>govárival</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he often used to say; he would often say</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">skazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вор</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">góvor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govorítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***говно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a> (7985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*govьno</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govnó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говна́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>го́вна</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>го́вен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shit, shitass, turd <i>(worthless person)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> crap, junk <i>(worthless thing)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable<span class="ib-comma">,</span> vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bullshit <i>(nonsense)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собачий.html>соба́чье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>govnó</b> sobáčʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dog shit (person or thing)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>Своё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вонять.html>воня́ет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svojó <b>govnó</b> ne vonjájet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">One’s own shit doesn’t stink!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говно.html>говно́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вонять.html>воня́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne trónʹ <b>govnó</b>, a to vonjátʹ búdet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Don't touch shit, because it will smell!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">гомно́</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gomnó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерьмо.html>дерьмо́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">derʹmó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кал.html>кал</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kal</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экскремент.html>экскреме́нты</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ekskreménty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кака́шки</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kakáški</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">фека́лии</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">fekálii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i>inoffensive</i>)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дрянь.html>дрянь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">drjanʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отброс.html>отбро́сы</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otbrósy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вор</a> (11473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*govorъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">góvor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́вора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́воры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говор.html>го́воров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the sound of talking, the sound of voices, the sound of speech</li>
<li>murmur</li>
<li>dialect, patois</li>
<li>pronunciation, accent</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́вшийся</a> (1464)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***говорить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a> (53)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*govoriti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gow(H)-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to call, cry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gaworzyć</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">hovořit</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">говорити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hovoryty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">гово̀рити</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govorítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поговорить.html>поговори́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to speak, to talk
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говорю́</a></b> по-ру́сски.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>govorjú</b> po-rússki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I <b>speak</b> Russian.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to say, to tell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>Что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Što oná <b>govorít</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What <b>is</b> she <b>saying</b>?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***говориться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́ться</a> (1464)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govorítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">expressing something to talk about</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:говориться.html>говори́тся</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пословица.html>посло́вице</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>govorítsja</b> (v poslóvice)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">as they say, as the saying goes</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорливый.html>говорли́вый</a> (22060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">govorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ли́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорливый.html>говорли́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">govorlívyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)говорли́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)говорли́вей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>talkative, chatty, loquacious, garrulous</li>
<li>boisterous, noisy <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a crowd</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>burbling, babbling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> beef

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:говяжий.html>говя́жье</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сало.html>са́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>govjážʹje</b> sálo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>beef</b> fat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:говяжий.html>говя́жье</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>govjážʹje</b> sérdce</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>beef</b> heart</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:говяжий.html>говя́жья</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:требуха.html>требуха́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>govjážʹja</b> trebuxá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>beef</b> offals</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гогот.html>го́гот</a> (26611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гоготать.html>гогота́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gogotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гогот.html>го́гот</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gógot</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гогот.html>го́гота</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гогот.html>го́готы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гогот.html>го́готов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(sound of a goose)</i> cackle, honk</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loud laughter, roars of laughter, guffaw</li></ol>

***гоготать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гоготать.html>гогота́ть</a> (16110)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гоготать.html>гогота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gogotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cackle <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of geese</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to roar with laughter</li></ol>

***год.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a> (49)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">годъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">godŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time, period, year, age</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*godъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">suitable time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰodʰo-</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰedʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to unite, be associated, be suitable</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p><p>Cognates include
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">годі</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hodi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enough</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́де</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gode</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ever</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (as in <span class="Cyrl" lang="bg">кой-годе</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="tr Latn">koj-gode</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> = whoever),
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">hod</i>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gody</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">yearly feast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Upper_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Upper Sorbian language">Upper Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="hsb">hody</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Christmas</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lower_Sorbian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lower Sorbian language">Lower Sorbian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">gódy</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Christmas</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">gadigs</i>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Gatte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">husband</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gätlich</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">convenient</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gegade</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gade</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gading</i>,
as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">gather</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">good</i>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gader</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">goed</i>,
and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">gut</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">god</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́ды</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лета́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>годо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>year
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">iz góda v god</i> ― <span class="e-translation">year in and year out, from year to year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>году́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v étom <b>godú</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">this year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">godámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">for years; for years on end</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:девяностый.html>девяно́стые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́ды</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">devjanóstyje <b>gódy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the '90s</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учебный.html>уче́бный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">učébnyj <b>god</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">school year; academic year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nóvyj <b>god</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">New Year’s Day</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú dvádcatʹ odín <b>god</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is 21 years old.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú dvádcatʹ tri <b>góda</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is 23 years old.<i></i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú dvádcatʹ pjatʹ let.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He is 25 years old.<i></i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сяча</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девятьсот.html>девятьсо́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девяносто.html>девяно́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">týsjača devjatʹsót devjanósto vtorój <b>god</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(year) 1992 (<i>in words</i>)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сячи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одиннадцатый.html>оди́ннадцатый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dve týsjači odínnadcatyj <b>god</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">(year) 2011 (<i>in words</i>)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́дом</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s káždym <b>gódom</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from year to year, year by year, year after year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнение.html>сравне́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:период.html>пери́одом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлого</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po sravnéniju s tém že períodom próšlovo <b>góda</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">as compared to the corresponding period last year, from the same time last year</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>When the genitive plural is needed after a (cardinal) number, the word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">let</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (the genitive plural of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, meaning summer) is used instead of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>годо́в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">godóv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This applies to numbers whose names do not end in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (2), <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (3), or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četýre</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (4) when in nominative, genitive, or accusative case (so this includes numbers like 114 whose name in Russian does not end in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></i>), as well as to numbers ending in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">četýre</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in genitive case.</li></ul>
<ul><li>To put this in another way, when a number should be followed by a nominative or genitive <b>singular</b>, the appropriate form of <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">god</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> is used. When a number should be followed by a <b>genitive plural</b>, the form <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">let</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> is used. When the number is in the dative, instrumental, or prepositional case, the appropriate form of <b><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">god</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> must be used. Examples: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b> (nominative singular), <b><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></b> (genitive singular), <b><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></b> (genitive singular), <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b> (genitive plural); but <b>бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>трёх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b> (genitive plural), <b>бо́льше <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пяти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a></b> (genitive plural); and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пяти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года́м</a></b> (dative plural), <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пятью́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года́ми</a></b> (instrumental plural), <b>o <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пяти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года́х</a></b> (prepositional plural).</li></ul>
<ul><li>When used with an ordinal number, the above rules don't apply, and one simply uses the needed form of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></b>, for example, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начало.html>нача́ле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девяностый.html>девяно́стых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>годо́в</a></b> ("At the beginning of the '90s")</li></ul>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:единица.html>единица</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измерение.html>измере́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:определяемый.html>определя́емая</a> астрономически <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>ра́вная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:период.html>пери́оду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращение.html>обраще́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вокруг.html>вокру́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звезда.html>звезды</a> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:частный.html>ча́стном</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чае</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>Земли</a> — 365 <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> 366 <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дней</a></i>) <span style="display: none"></span> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:пройти.html>Прошло́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>после</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:этот.html>э́той</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поездка.html>пое́здки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>года</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мые</a> счастливейшие <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пролететь.html>пролете́ли</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часа</a>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>

***годиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>годи́ться</a> (3318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*godìti sę</i>. Synchronically as if from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">годи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">godítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>годи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">godítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сгодиться.html>сгоди́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригодиться.html>пригоди́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suit</li>
<li>to be fit (for), to be of use
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:никуда.html>никуда́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>годи́тся</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Éto (nikudá) ne <b>godítsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's no good (at all).</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:годиться.html>годи́тся</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On tebé v otcý <b>godítsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He's old enough to be your father! (reproach)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригодный.html>приго́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prigódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дность</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gódnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***годность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дность</a> (30274)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">го́днасць</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">hódnascʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and, more distantly, with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">goodness</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gódnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fitness (of something for some purpose), suitability; validity</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негодный.html>него́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">negódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пригодный.html>приго́дный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prigódnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***годный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a> (10105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*godьnъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʰedʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to unite, be associated, suit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">good</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годный.html>го́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gódnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)годне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)годне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fit, suitable, well-suited, valid, apposite, appropriate, relevant <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + genitive or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, for/to something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:годность.html>го́дность</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gódnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<tbody><tr>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Полторашники, которым <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">годки</span> уже предоставляют многие послабления в манере поведения и в форме одежды, обязаны заставлять карасей и духов «шуршать» (то есть, выполнять все «грязные» работы по кораблю). </span></li>
</ul></li>

***голень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голень.html>го́лень</a> (16265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">голѣнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golěnĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:голень.html>го́лень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">golenĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golěnь</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golenь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">naked</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голень.html>го́лень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gólenʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голень.html>го́лени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голень.html>го́лени</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голень.html>го́леней</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">голя́шка</b>)

***голова.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a> (92)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*golva</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*GelH-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">callow</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глава.html>глава́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glavá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Church Slavonicism).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golová</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́ловы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>head
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>golový</b> do nóg</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from <b>head</b> to foot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пята.html>пя́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>golový</b> do pját</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from <b>head</b> to toe</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mind; brains
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:даже.html>да́же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голове́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá étovo dáže i v <b>golové</b> né bylo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I didn’t have it on my mind either.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">golová</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>головы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>го́ловы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>head; chief; master
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:городской.html>городско́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gorodskój <b>golová</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">mayor</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сам.html>сам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sam sebé <b>golová</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">one’s own master</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:желтый.html>Жёлтая</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:сырой.html>сыра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочиться.html>сочи́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:искрящийся.html>искрящимся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хрустальный.html>хруста́льным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:колпак.html>колпако́м</a>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
